# Generate graph fuel & speed

## Request Header (alway pass : token)

# getFuelGraphByDevice

## url
    http://{server}/api/report/getFuelGraphByDevice

## request body
```json
{
    "devices": [
        {"device_id":18681}
    ],
    "start_date": "04-02-2019 00:00",
    "end_date": "06-02-2019 23:00"
}
```
